### [1] [AIS: Adaptive Importance Sampling for Quantized RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13907)
*Jiajun Zhou,Wei Shao,Lingchao Zheng,Yuwei Fan,Ngai Wong*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型强化学习中使用低精度 rollout（FP8）带来的训练- rollout 不匹配问题，本文提出自适应重要性采样（AIS），通过每批次动态调整混合系数来抑制不稳定偏差同时保留探索增益，在数学推理和规划基准上匹配 BF16 基线并保持 1.5–2.76 倍 rollout 加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型强化学习受限于 rollout 生成的计算成本，促使使用低精度（FP8）rollout 配合 BF16 训练器以提升吞吐量并降低内存压力，但这引入了 rollout-训练不匹配，会偏置策略梯度甚至导致训练崩溃。

Method: 提出自适应重要性采样（AIS），融合三种实时诊断指标（权重可靠性、发散严重性、方差放大）生成单一混合系数，在未校正梯度与完全重要性加权梯度之间插值，抑制不匹配中的不稳定偏差成分同时保留探索收益。

Result: 将 AIS 集成到 GRPO 中，在 LLaDA-8B-Instruct、Qwen3-8B 和 Qwen3.5-9B 上的数学推理与规划基准中，AIS 在多数任务上匹配 BF16 基线表现，同时保持 FP8 带来的 1.5 到 2.76 倍 rollout 加速。

Conclusion: 低精度 rollout 的不匹配具有双重效应（早期探索增益 vs. 后期不稳定偏差），AIS 能有效解耦这两种效应，在保持加速的同时恢复训练稳定性与性能。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models (LLMs) is dominated by the cost of rollout generation, which has motivated the use of low-precision rollouts (e.g., FP8) paired with a BF16 trainer to improve throughput and reduce memory pressure. This introduces a rollout-training mismatch that biases the policy gradient and can cause training to collapse outright on reasoning benchmarks. We show that the mismatch is non-stationary and acts as a double-edged sword: early in training it provides a stochastic exploration bonus, exposing the gradient to trajectories the trainer would otherwise under-sample, but the same perturbation transitions into a destabilizing source of bias as the policy concentrates.
  To solve this, we propose Adaptive Importance Sampling (AIS), a correction framework that adjusts the strength of its intervention on a per-batch basis. AIS combines three real-time diagnostics, namely weight reliability, divergence severity, and variance amplification, into a single mixing coefficient that interpolates between the uncorrected and fully importance-weighted gradients, suppressing the destabilizing component of the mismatch while preserving its exploratory benefit. We integrate AIS into GRPO and evaluate it on the diffusion-based LLaDA-8B-Instruct and the autoregressive Qwen3-8B and Qwen3.5-9B across mathematical reasoning and planning benchmarks. AIS matches the BF16 baseline on most tasks while retaining the 1.5 to 2.76x rollout speedup of FP8.

</details>


### [2] [Covariance-aware sampling for Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13910)
*Andrea Schioppa,Tim Salimans*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 提出一种协方差感知采样器，通过结构化傅里叶空间协方差分解，在少步数设定下提升像素空间扩散模型的采样质量，仅需额外一次JVP计算即可超越现有二阶采样器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有采样器在少步数设定下效果不佳，因为仅依赖逆过程预测均值而忽略了协方差信息。

Method: 利用Tweedie公式估计协方差，结合结构化傅里叶空间分解协方差矩阵，作为DDIM扩展实现，每步仅增加一次雅可比-向量乘积(JVP)计算。

Result: 在相同NFE下，始终优于Heun、DPM-Solver++等二阶采样器及aDDIM采样器。

Conclusion: 显式建模逆过程协方差能有效提升少步数生成质量，且计算开销极小。

Abstract: We present a covariance-aware sampler that improves the quality of pixel-space Diffusion Model (DM) sampling in the few-step regime. We hypothesize that in the few-step regime samplers fail because they rely solely on the predicted mean of the reverse distribution, while our solution explicitly models the reverse-process covariance. Our method combines Tweedie's formula to estimate the covariance with an efficient, structured Fourier-space decomposition of the covariance matrix. Implemented as an extension of DDIM, our method requires only a minimal overhead: one extra Jacobian-Vector Product (JVP) per step. We demonstrate that for pixel-based DMs, our method consistently produces superior samples compared to state-of-the-art second order samplers (Heun, DPM-Solver++) and the recent aDDIM sampler, at an identical number of function evaluations (NFE).

</details>


### [3] [A Survey on Data-Dependent Worst-Case Generalization Bounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13913)
*Hubert Leroux,Jean Marcus,Julien Roger*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文综述了深度学习过参数化背景下非平凡泛化保证的最新进展，围绕三个核心步骤展开：扩展PAC-Bayesian理论到随机数据相关假设集、利用优化轨迹的几何与拓扑描述符细化复杂度项、用稳定性假设替代信息论项，并通过统一模板不等式和边界对比进行整合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习模型严重过参数化却仍能良好泛化，与基于固定假设空间上一致收敛的经典学习理论相矛盾。整个参数空间的一致边界在此情况下是空洞的，因此需要关注算法实际访问的参数空间部分来恢复非平凡保证。

Method: 1) 将PAC-Bayesian理论扩展到随机、数据相关的假设集（arXiv:2404.17442）；2) 利用优化轨迹的几何和拓扑描述符（分形维数、α加权寿命和、正幅度等）细化复杂度项（arXiv:2006.09313, arXiv:2302.02766, arXiv:2407.08723）；3) 用稳定性假设替代信息论项（arXiv:2507.06775）。最终通过统一模板不等式和边界对比进行整合。

Result: 形成了一个统一的模板不等式框架，并对上述方法导出的边界进行了头对头比较。

Conclusion: 该综述系统地组织并统一了围绕算法访问参数空间而非整个假设空间来建立非平凡泛化保证的研究路线，为理解深度学习泛化提供了更紧致的理论工具。

Abstract: Deep neural networks generalize well despite being heavily overparameterized, in apparent contradiction with classical learning theory based on uniform convergence over fixed hypothesis spaces. Uniform bounds over the entire parameter space are vacuous in this regime, and recent work has shown that non-vacuous guarantees can be recovered by restricting attention to the part of parameter space that the algorithm actually visits. This survey paper organizes this line of work around three steps: extending PAC-Bayesian theory to random, data-dependent hypothesis sets (arXiv:2404.17442); refining the complexity term with geometric and topological descriptors of the optimization trajectory, including fractal dimensions, alpha-weighted lifetime sums, and positive magnitude (arXiv:2006.09313, arXiv:2302.02766, arXiv:2407.08723); and replacing the resulting information-theoretic terms by stability assumptions (arXiv:2507.06775). We unify these contributions around a single template inequality and a head-to-head comparison of the resulting bounds.

</details>


### [4] [Multi-Scale Dequant: Eliminating Dequantization Bottleneck via Activation Decomposition for Efficient LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13915)
*Lingchao Zheng,Yuwei Fan,Jun Li,Chengqiu Hu,Qichen Liao,Junyi Fan,Rui Shi,Fangzheng Miao*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出多尺度分解量化框架（MSD），通过将高精度激活分解为多个低精度分量直接与量化权重相乘，消除了LLM推理中权重/KV反量化的计算瓶颈，在Ascend NPU等架构上避免了反量化导致的向量-立方流水线停滞，并实现KV缓存HBM流量降低2.5倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现代AI加速器（如Ascend NPU）上，反量化操作（将低比特权重转换回高精度）已成为LLM推理的关键瓶颈，其消耗的计算周期甚至超过矩阵乘法本身，导致高吞吐张量核心利用率不足。

Method: MSD不再将低比特权重提升至BF16精度，而是将高精度BF16激活分解为多个低精度分量，每个分量通过原生硬件加速的GEMM直接与量化权重相乘。从精度转换范式转向多尺度近似，支持INT8和MXFP4两种权重格式并推导了严格误差界。

Result: 对于W4A16的INT8权重，两遍INT8分解达到近16有效比特；对于MXFP4权重，两遍分解达到近6.6有效比特（误差界1/64），超越单遍MXFP8（5.24比特）且保持相同GEMM计算时间。KV缓存HBM流量降低2.5倍，数值仿真表明精度不退化甚至L2误差更低。

Conclusion: MSD通过消除反量化操作在解耦计算架构上的流水线停滞，有效提升LLM推理效率，在保持精度的同时显著降低延迟和内存带宽需求。

Abstract: Quantization is essential for efficient large language model (LLM) inference, yet the dequantization step-converting low-bit weights back to high-precision for matrix multiplication has become a critical bottleneck on modern AI accelerators. On architectures with decoupled compute units (e.g., Ascend NPUs), dequantization operations can consume more cycles than the matrix multiplication itself, leaving the high-throughput tensor cores underutilized. This paper presents Multi-Scale Dequant (MSD), a quantization framework that removes weight/KV dequantization from the GEMM critical path. Instead of lifting low-bit weights to BF16 precision, MSD decomposes high-precision BF16 activations into multiple low-precision components, each of which can be multiplied directly with quantized weights via native hardware-accelerated GEMM. This approach shifts the computational paradigm from precision conversion to multi-scale approximation, avoiding INT8-to-BF16 weight conversion before GEMM. We instantiate MSD for two weight formats and derive tight error bounds for each. For INT8 weights (W4A16), two-pass INT8 decomposition achieves near 16 effective bits. For MXFP4 weights (W4A16), two-pass MXFP4 decomposition yields near 6.6 effective bits with error bound 1/64 per block surpassing single-pass MXFP8(5.24 bits) while maintaining the same effective GEMM compute time. We further derive closed-form latency and HBM traffic models showing that MSD avoids the Vector-Cube pipeline stall caused by dequantization and reduces KV cache HBM traffic by up to 2.5 times in attention. Numerical simulations on matrix multiplication and Flash Attention kernels confirm that MSD does not degrade accuracy compared to dequantization baselines, and in many settings achieves lower L2 error.

</details>


### [5] [A Regret Perspective on Online Multiple Testing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13916)
*Qingyang Hao,Kongchang Zhou,Fang Kong,Hongxin Wei*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文针对在线多重检验（OMT）中假阳性与假阴性成本不对称的问题，提出加权遗憾（Weighted Regret）统一评估框架，并揭示遗憾守恒对偶性：严格FDR控制的确定性过程必然遭受Ω(T)线性遗憾。为此提出Decoupled-OMT（DOMT）元包装器，通过历史解耦的随机扰动缓解阈值枯竭，实现Ω(√T)阶最优遗憾降低，并在非平稳环境中导航Pareto前沿。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统OMT方法孤立评估FDR与统计功效，忽视了现代自动化流程中假阳性和假阴性成本的高度不对称性，缺乏统一量化框架来权衡这两种错误。

Method: 提出加权遗憾指标统一评估OMT性能；证明遗憾守恒对偶性定理；设计Decoupled-OMT（DOMT）元包装器，通过历史解耦的非负随机扰动机制缓解阈值枯竭。

Result: DOMT在平稳环境中保持精确渐近安全性，严格界定了冷启动期间的有限样本误差膨胀；在突发性环境中实现Ω(√T)遗憾降低，并导出"冷启动税"刻画算法优越性的精确相变。

Conclusion: DOMT一致性地缩减经验加权遗憾，实现阈值枯竭的阶最优次线性缓解，有助于在非平稳条件下导航OMT的Pareto最优前沿。

Abstract: Online Multiple Testing (OMT), a fundamental pillar of sequential statistical inference, traditionally evaluates the False Discovery Rate (FDR) and statistical power in isolation, obscuring the highly asymmetric costs of false positives and false negatives in modern automated pipelines. To unify this evaluation, we introduce $\textit{Weighted Regret}$. Under this metric, we prove the $\textit{Duality of Regret Conservation}$: purely deterministic procedures ensuring strict FDR control inevitably incur an $Ω(T)$ linear regret penalty, as threshold depletion during signal-sparse cold starts forces massive false negatives. Tailored for exogenous testing streams, we propose Decoupled-OMT (DOMT) as a baseline-agnostic meta-wrapper. By incorporating a history-decoupled, strictly non-negative random perturbation, DOMT rescues purely deterministic baselines from severe threshold depletion. Crucially, it preserves exact asymptotic safety in stationary environments and rigorously bounds finite-sample error inflation during cold-starts. Guaranteeing zero additional false negatives, it yields an order-optimal $Ω(\sqrt{T})$ regret reduction in bursty environments, with a derived ``Cold-Start Tax'' characterizing the exact phase transition of algorithmic superiority. Experiments validate that DOMT consistently curtails empirical weighted regret, achieving an order-optimal sublinear mitigation of threshold depletion to navigate the non-stationary Pareto frontier.

</details>


### [6] [Pause and Reflect: Conformal Aggregation for Chain-of-Thought Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14098)
*Yu Gu,Zijun Yu,Vahid Partovi Nia,Masoud Asgharian*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于共形预测的链式思维推理方法，通过加权评分聚合替代多数投票，并校准弃权规则，在有限样本下保证系统回答时的错误率受控，实现了高选择性准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在CoT推理中，自一致性方法通过聚合多条推理路径提升性能，但聚合不确定性成为核心挑战——错误自信回答的代价远高于弃权。现有多数投票策略无法提供统计保证。

Method: 用加权评分聚合替代多数投票；引入共形风险控制校准弃权规则；识别评分可分性作为弃权可证明提升准确率的关键条件；推导出仅凭校准数据即可预测准确率提升的闭式表达式。

Result: 在4个基准、4个开源模型、3类评分上，实际自信错误率与预设目标一致；在GSM8K上弃权不到5%即达到90.1%选择性准确率，而多数投票基线为82%。

Conclusion: 该方法为纯推理时方法，无需重新训练，能有效控制聚合不确定性下的自信错误率，显著优于多数投票基线。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning with self-consistency improves performance by aggregating multiple sampled reasoning paths. In this setting, correctness is no longer tied to a single reasoning trace but to the aggregation rule over a pool of candidate paths, making aggregation uncertainty the central challenge. This issue is critical where confidently incorrect answers are far more costly than abstentions. We introduce a conformal procedure for CoT reasoning that directly addresses aggregation uncertainty. Our approach replaces majority voting with weighted score aggregation over reasoning paths and calibrates an abstention rule using conformal risk control. This approach leads to finite-sample guarantees on the confident-error rate--the probability that the system answers and is wrong. We further identify score separability as the key condition under which abstention provably improves selective accuracy, and derive closed-form expressions that predict accuracy gains from calibration data alone. The method is fully inference-time, and requires no retraining. Across four benchmarks, four open-source models, and three score classes, realized confident-error rates are consistent with the prescribed targets up to calibration-split and test-set variability. Our method achieves $90.1\%$ selective accuracy on GSM8K by abstaining on less than $5\%$ of problems, compared with $82\%$ accuracy under majority-voting baseline.

</details>


### [7] [To discretize continually: Mean shift interacting particle systems for Bayesian inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14142)
*Ayoub Belhadji,Daniel Sharp,Youssef M. Marzouk*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过最小化最大均值差异（MMD）的交互粒子系统来构建加权样本集（求积规则）的新方法，用于近似未知归一化概率分布的期望。该方法扩展了均值漂移算法和最优量化算法，具有归一化常数不变性，支持无梯度和基于梯度的实现，能够快速收敛、处理各向异性和多模态、避免模式崩溃，并适用于高维问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 贝叶斯推断及其他领域中，针对仅知未归一化密度的概率分布进行期望积分是一项核心任务，现有方法在效率、可扩展性和对复杂分布（如多模态、各向异性）的适应性上存在不足。

Method: 通过构建交互粒子系统来最小化与目标分布之间的最大均值差异（MMD），从而生成加权样本（求积规则）。该方法将经典均值漂移算法和最优量化算法扩展到连续分布情形，并设计了不依赖未知归一化常数的动力学系统，同时提供无梯度和基于梯度的两种实现版本。

Result: 所提方法在多种基准采样问题（包括多模态混合分布、贝叶斯层次模型、PDE约束反问题等）上表现出快速收敛、能够捕捉各向异性和多模态性、避免模式崩溃，并且可扩展到高维空间。

Conclusion: 基于MMD最小化的均值漂移交互粒子系统为贝叶斯推断中的期望近似提供了一种高效、鲁棒且可扩展的新框架，兼具理论优美性和实际应用价值。

Abstract: Integration against a probability distribution given its unnormalized density is a central task in Bayesian inference and other fields. We introduce new methods for approximating such expectations with a small set of weighted samples -- i.e., a quadrature rule -- constructed via an interacting particle system that minimizes maximum mean discrepancy (MMD) to the target distribution. These methods extend the classical mean shift algorithm, as well as recent algorithms for optimal quantization of empirical distributions, to the case of continuous distributions. Crucially, our approach creates dynamics for MMD minimization that are invariant to the unknown normalizing constant; they also admit both gradient-free and gradient-informed implementations. The resulting mean shift interacting particle systems converge quickly, capture anisotropy and multi-modality, avoid mode collapse, and scale to high dimensions. We demonstrate their performance on a wide range of benchmark sampling problems, including multi-modal mixtures, Bayesian hierarchical models, PDE-constrained inverse problems, and beyond.

</details>


### [8] [On the Burden of Achieving Fairness in Conformal Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14260)
*Ziang Gao,Pengqi Liu,Archer Yi Yang,Mouloud Belbahri,Jesse C. Cresswell,Masoud Asgharian*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文揭示了分裂共形预测中 pooled 校准会隐藏组间分数分布异质性，导致组间覆盖率失真；证明了 Equalized Coverage 和 Equalized Set Size 两种公平定义之间存在根本性张力；量化了分组策略与混合策略之间的权衡代价；实验验证了校准选择不会消除异质性，而是决定失真出现在覆盖率还是集合大小维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共形预测常使用单一的 pooled 阈值进行校准，但这种方法可能掩盖不同组之间的分数分布异质性，从而导致组间覆盖率出现扭曲。作者希望从理论层面理解这一现象，并探究不同公平定义之间的权衡关系。

Method: 从分裂共形校准背后的总体分数分布出发，推导了守恒定律和下界，证明 pooled 校准会导致不可约的组间覆盖率失真；证明了 Equalized Coverage 和 Equalized Set Size 两种公平定义存在根本性矛盾；量化了分组策略与混合策略之间的移动成本；通过合成数据和真实数据进行了有限样本实验验证。

Result: 推导出 pooled 校准会不可避免地产生跨组分位数异质性所决定的覆盖率失真；证明 Equalized Coverage 与 Equalized Set Size 两种公平定义本质上不可兼得；发现校准选择并不消除组间异质性，而是将失真分配到覆盖率或集合大小两个维度之一。

Conclusion: 校准选择无法消除跨组异质性，只能决定异质性导致的失真出现在哪个维度（覆盖率或集合大小），为实践中面向公平性的校准选择提供了理论分析框架。

Abstract: Conformal prediction is often calibrated with a single pooled threshold, but this can hide cross-group heterogeneity in score distributions and distort group-wise coverage. We study this phenomenon through the population score distributions underlying split conformal calibration. First, we derive a conservation law and lower bound showing that pooled calibration incurs irreducible group-wise coverage distortion at a scale set by cross-group quantile heterogeneity. Second, we demonstrate that the two leading fairness definitions for conformal prediction, Equalized Coverage and Equalized Set Size, are fundamentally in tension. Third, we quantify the cost of moving between policies which treat groups separately or pool them. Experiments on synthetic and real data confirm the same bidirectional trade-off after finite-sample calibration. Our results show that, for the policy families studied here, calibration choice does not remove cross-group heterogeneity; it determines whether the resulting distortion appears in the coverage or size dimension, providing a principled lens for analyzing fairness-oriented calibration choices in practice.

</details>


### [9] [Training-Free Generative Sampling via Moment-Matched Score Smoothing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14276)
*Zhenyu Yao,Daniel Paulin*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 提出MM-SOLD，一种无需训练、基于矩匹配的交互式粒子采样器，通过沿采样轨迹强制目标矩来替代昂贵的神经扩散模型训练，在大粒子极限下证明粒子密度收敛到与训练数据经验矩一致的吉布斯-玻尔兹曼分布，在2D分布和潜空间图像生成任务上达到与神经扩散基线竞争的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经扩散模型训练计算成本高昂，而分数匹配隐式平滑经验分数产生的平滑偏差有助于泛化；本文旨在设计一种无需训练的替代方案，通过矩匹配实现类似效果。

Method: 提出MM-SOLD（矩匹配分数平滑过阻尼朗之万动力学），一种无需训练的交互式粒子采样器，在采样轨迹中强制目标矩；通过大粒子极限分析证明经验粒子密度收敛到确定性极限，其单粒子平稳边际为对朴素分数平滑扩散目标进行指数倾斜得到的吉布斯-玻尔兹曼密度，且该分布的均值和协方差与训练数据经验矩一致。

Result: 在2D分布和潜空间图像生成实验中，MM-SOLD在CPU上实现快速、鲁棒、无需训练的采样，样本保真度和多样性与神经扩散基线相当。

Conclusion: MM-SOLD作为一种无需训练的替代方案，通过矩匹配机制有效捕捉数据分布的低维几何结构，在计算效率和采样质量之间取得了良好平衡。

Abstract: Diffusion models generate samples by denoising along the score of a perturbed target distribution. In practice, one trains a neural diffusion model, which is computationally expensive. Recent work suggests that score matching implicitly smooths the empirical score, and that this smoothing bias promotes generalization by capturing low-dimensional data geometry. We propose moment-matched score-smoothed overdamped Langevin dynamics (MM-SOLD), a training-free interacting particle sampler that enforces the target moments throughout the sampling trajectory. We prove that, in the large-particle limit, the empirical particle density converges to a deterministic limit whose one-particle stationary marginal is a Gibbs--Boltzmann density obtained by exponentially tilting a naive score-smoothed diffusion target. The mean and covariance of this distribution agree with the empirical moments of the training data. Experiments on 2D distributions and latent-space image generation show that MM-SOLD enables fast, robust, training-free sampling on CPUs, with sample fidelity and diversity competitive with neural diffusion baselines.

</details>


### [10] [Large Dimensional Kernel Ridge Regression: Extending to Product Kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14524)
*Yang Zhou,Yicheng Li,Yuqian Cheng,Qian Lin*

Main category: stat.ML

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于大维核岭回归中饱和效应和多重下降行为的研究多局限于球面上的内积核函数或强特征函数假设（如超收缩性），这些现象是否适用于其他核函数仍是一个开放问题。

Result: 恢复了三类关键现象：1) 源条件s≤1时的极小最优性；2) s>1时的饱和效应；3) 收敛率中的周期平台现象以及随样本量n变化的多重下降行为。

Abstract: Recent studies have reported $\textit{saturation effects}$ and $\textit{multiple descent behavior}$ in large dimensional kernel ridge regression (KRR). However, these findings are predominantly derived under restrictive settings, such as inner product kernels on sphere or strong eigenfunction assumptions like hypercontractivity. Whether such behaviors hold for other kernels remains an open question. In this paper, we establish a broad, new family of large dimensional kernels and derive the corresponding convergence rates of the generalization error. As a result, we recover key phenomena previously associated with inner product kernels on sphere, including: $i)$ the $\textit{minimax optimality}$ when the source condition $s\le 1$; $ii)$ the $\textit{saturation effect}$ when $s>1$; $iii)$ a $\textit{periodic plateau phenomenon}$ in the convergence rate and a $\textit {multiple-descent behavior}$ with respect to the sample size $n$.

### [11] [Scaling Laws from Sequential Feature Recovery: A Solvable Hierarchical Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14567)

Motivation: 理解尺度定律（scaling laws）在深度学习中的出现机制，特别是从特征学习（feature learning）角度解释多层网络如何随着数据量增加而呈现幂律衰减的预测误差。

Method: 构建高维层次化目标函数（组合潜在特征，权重幂律衰减），提出逐层谱算法；利用随机矩阵理论和基于预解式的扰动分析推导特征恢复的精确阈值和误差上/下界。

Abstract: We propose a simple mechanism by which scaling laws emerge from feature learning in multi-layer networks. We study a high-dimensional hierarchical target that is a globally high-degree function, but that can be represented by a combination of latent compositional features whose weights decrease as a power law. We show that a layer-wise spectral algorithm adapted to this compositional structure achieves improved scaling relative to shallow, non-adaptive methods, and recovers the latent directions sequentially: strong features become detectable at small sample sizes, while weaker features require more data. We prove sharp feature-wise recovery thresholds and show that aggregating these transitions yields an explicit power-law decay of the prediction error. Technically, the analysis relies on random matrix methods and a resolvent-based perturbation argument, which gives matching upper and lower bounds for individual eigenvector recovery beyond what standard gap-based perturbation bounds provide. Numerical experiments confirm the predicted sequential recovery, finite-size smoothing of the thresholds, and separation from non-hierarchical kernel baselines. Together, these results show how smooth scaling laws can emerge from a cascade of sharp feature-learning transitions.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有函数型数据聚类方法过度侧重划分精度而忽视可解释性，当数据生成过程具有特定底层结构且簇间存在序数关系时，难以提取有意义的洞见。

The proposed method is evaluated through simulations and real-world applications. These curves represent changes in reflected light intensity over time at multiple measurement spots with immobilized antigens during analyte exposure, capturing the binding dynamics of the system. The goal is to identify intrinsic signal patterns solely from the observed dynamics, making this dataset an ideal benchmark for assessing the added interpretability of the proposed approach. ### [13] [Average Gradient Outer Product in kernel regression provably recovers the central subspace for multi-index models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15082)
*Libin Zhu,Damek Davis,Dmitriy Drusvyatskiy,Maryam Fazel*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文研究核岭回归（KRR）结合平均梯度外积（AGOP）在样本量远低于准确预测所需时，仍能可靠恢复低维中心子空间的问题，证明了预测与表示之间存在分离，并解释了递归特征机（RFM）等迭代核方法在实践中的样本效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在样本量不足以实现准确预测的情况下，学习器是否仍能发现数据中有用的低维结构，即预测与表示之间是否存在分离现象。

Method: 对数据拟合核岭回归（KRR），然后从拟合的预测器中计算平均梯度外积（AGOP），并证明在合理假设下，AGOP的前r维特征空间能够可靠地恢复中心子空间。

Result: 当目标函数f*的低p度分量已包含所有相关预测方向时，子空间恢复所需的样本量为n≍d^{p+δ}（任意δ∈(0,1)），远低于KRR实现准确预测所需的n≍d^{p*}样本量。

Conclusion: 预测与表示之间存在本质分离：子空间恢复比准确预测需要更少的样本；该结果为RFM等迭代核方法的样本效率提供了理论解释。

Abstract: We study a prototypical situation when a learned predictor can discover useful low-dimensional structure in data, while using fewer samples than are needed for accurate prediction. Specifically, we consider the problem of recovering a multi-index polynomial $f^*(x)=h(Ux)$, with $U\in\mathbb{R}^{r\times d}$ and $r\ll d$, from finitely many data/label pairs. Importantly, the target function depends on input $x$ only through the projection onto an unknown $r$-dimensional central subspace. The algorithm we analyze is appealingly simple: fit kernel ridge regression (KRR) to the data and compute the Average Gradient Outer Product (AGOP) from the fitted predictor. Our main results show that under reasonable assumptions the top $r$-dimensional eigenspace of AGOP provably recovers the central subspace, even in regimes when the prediction error remains large. Specifically, if the target function $f^*$ has degree $p^*$, it is known that $n\asymp d^{p^*}$ samples are necessary for KRR to achieve accurate prediction. In contrast, we show that if a low degree $p$ component of $f^*$ already carries all relevant directions for prediction, subspace recovery occurs in the much lower sample regime $n\asymp d^{p+δ}$ for any $δ\in(0,1)$. Our results thus demonstrate a separation between prediction and representation, and provide an explanation for why iterative kernel methods such as Recursive Feature Machines (RFM) can be sample-efficient in practice.

The LP solution is mathematically correct, but simplifications are made in the model, and data supply errors may occur. Therefore, further insight is needed to trust the results.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Off-policy evaluation (OPE) estimates the value of a target treatment policy (e.g., a recommender system) using data collected by a different logging policy. It enables high-stakes experimentation without live deployment, yet in practice accuracy depends heavily on the logging policy used to collect data for computing the estimate. We study how to design logging policies that minimize OPE error for given target policies. We characterize a fundamental reward-coverage tradeoff: concentrating probability mass on high-reward actions reduces variance but risks missing signal on actions the target policy may take. We propose a unifying framework for logging policy design and derive optimal policies in canonical informational regimes where the target policy and reward distribution are (i) known, (ii) unknown, and (iii) partially known through priors or noisy estimates at logging time. Our results provide actionable guidance for firms choosing among multiple candidate recommendation systems. We demonstrate the importance of treatment selection when gathering data for OPE, and describe theoretically optimal approaches when this is a firm's primary objective. We also distill practical design principles for selecting logging policies when operational constraints prevent implementing the theoretical optimum.

### [16] [RoSHAP: A Distributional Framework and Robust Metric for Stable Feature Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15154)
*Lanxin Xiang,Liang Shi,Youhui Ye,Boyu Jiang,Dawei Zhou,Feng Guo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 特征归因分析在解释机器学习模型时至关重要，但现有的归因指标存在随机波动问题——不同的训练-测试划分、随机种子或模型拟合过程会导致归因值和特征排名出现显著差异，影响结论的可靠性。

Method: 提出一个统计框架，对特征归因分数的分布进行建模，通过自举重采样(Bootstrap)和核密度估计(Kernel Density Estimation)来估计分布；证明在温和正则条件下，聚合后的特征归因分数渐近服从高斯分布，从而降低分布估计的计算成本；提出RoSHAP指标，综合奖励那些活跃、强且稳定的特征。

Result: 在模拟和真实数据实验中，RoSHAP在识别信号特征方面优于标准的单次运行归因指标；使用RoSHAP筛选的特征构建的模型，在预测性能上与全特征模型相当，但使用的预测因子大幅减少。

Conclusion: RoSHAP方法提升了机器学习模型的稳定性和可解释性，能够为分析提供可靠且一致的洞察。

Abstract: Feature attribution analysis is critical for interpreting machine learning models and supporting reliable data-driven decisions. However, feature attribution measures often exhibit stochastic variation: different train--test splits, random seeds, or model-fitting procedures can produce substantially different attribution values and feature rankings. This paper proposes a framework for incorporating stochastic nature of feature attribution and a robust attribution metric, RoSHAP, for stable feature ranking based on the SHAP metric. The proposed framework models the distribution of feature attribution scores and estimates it through bootstrap resampling and kernel density estimation. We show that, under mild regularity conditions, the aggregated feature attribution score is asymptotically Gaussian, which greatly reduces the computational cost of distribution estimation. The RoSHAP summarizes the distribution of SHAP into a robust feature-ranking criterion that simultaneously rewards features that are active, strong, and stable. Through simulations and real-data experiments, the proposed framework and RoSHAP outperform standard single-run attribution measures in identifying signal features. In addition, models built using RoSHAP-selected features achieve predictive performance comparable to full-feature models while using substantially fewer predictors. The proposed RoSHAP approach improves the stability and interpretability of machine learning models, enabling reliable and consistent insights for analysis.

### [17] [Vision-Based Runtime Monitoring under Varying Specifications using Semantic Latent Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13923)
*Bardh Hoxha,Oliver Schön,Hideki Okamoto,Lars Lindemann,Georgios Fainekos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在部分可观测条件下，基于视觉观测对过去时间信号时态逻辑（ptSTL）进行认证运行时监控。提出了一种可重用的监控框架，通过语义基（semantic basis）作为最小预测目标，结合单调1-Lipschitz可重用接口和一致性校准，实现对目标片段内任意公式的认证，无需针对每个公式重新训练。实验在行人交叉路口和Waymo数据集上验证了方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有监控方法在部分可观测环境下缺乏有限样本保障，且通常需要针对每个公式单独训练，缺乏可重用性。本文旨在设计一种可重用的、提供有限样本保证的运行时监控器。

Method: 1) 提出语义基（semantic basis）作为最小预测目标，证明其是单调1-Lipschitz可重用接口类中的最优选择；2) 设计基于解析树的确定性解码器评估任意公式；3) 采用单次一致性校准（conformal calibration）认证整个片段，无需联合界（union bound）；4) 提出滚动预测监控器（rolling prediction monitor），仅预测当前谓词值并在线重建时间历史。

Result: 在行人交叉路口基准上，滚动监控器在短时域上界更紧，语义基监控器在长时域上界紧致度高达4倍。在Waymo实车数据上，两种监控器均经验证满足一致性覆盖保证。

Conclusion: 提出的可重用监控框架能够在部分可观测条件下对ptSTL公式提供有限样本认证保证，语义基方法在长时域上表现更优，滚动方法在短时域上更紧致，两者在实际驾驶数据上均有效。

Abstract: We study certified runtime monitoring of past-time signal temporal logic (ptSTL) from visual observations under partial observability. The monitor must infer safety-relevant quantities from images and provide finite-sample guarantees, while being \emph{reusable}: once trained and calibrated, it should certify any formula in a target fragment without per-formula retraining. For fragments induced by a finite dictionary of temporal atoms, we prove that the \emph{semantic basis}, the vector of atom robustness scores, is the minimum prediction target within the class of monotone, 1-Lipschitz reusable interfaces: any formula is evaluated by a deterministic decoder derived from the parse tree, and a single conformal calibration pass certifies the entire fragment with no union bound. We also introduce a \emph{rolling prediction monitor} that predicts only current predicate values and reconstructs temporal history online; this is easier to learn but grows conservative at long horizons. On a pedestrian-crossroad benchmark, rolling achieves tighter certified bounds at short horizons while the semantic-basis monitor is up to 4-times tighter at long horizons. We validate the presented monitors on real-world Waymo driving data, where both monitors satisfy the conformal coverage guarantee empirically.

</details>


### [18] [Mechanistic Interpretability of EEG Foundation Models via Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13930)
*William Lehn-Schiøler,Magnus Ruud Kjær,Rahul Thapa,Magnus Guldberg Pedersen,Anton Storgaard Mosquera,Nick Williams,Radu Gatej,Tue Lehn-Schiøler,Sándor Beniczky,Sadasivan Puthusserypady,James Zou,Lars Kai Hansen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EEG基础模型在临床任务上表现优异，但其内部计算机制不透明，阻碍了临床信任。作者旨在通过机械可解释性方法揭开模型内部表征的黑箱。

Method: 使用TopK稀疏自编码器（SAEs）从三个架构各异的EEG Transformer（SleepFM、REVE、LaBraM）中提取稀疏特征字典；基于临床分类体系（异常、年龄、性别、用药）对特征进行基准测试，衡量单语义性和纠缠度；通过单一超参数程序（内在字典健康审计）跨架构迁移；引入"目标vs偏离目标"探测面积指标量化概念引导的选择性。

Result: 发现三种操作区间：选择性可控、编码但纠缠、未编码；暴露了"破坏球"干预（全局模型性能崩溃）和临床纠缠（如年龄-病理混杂无法分离）；频谱解码器将潜在操作映射为生理可解释的频率特征（如病理性慢波抑制和α频带恢复）。

Conclusion: 该框架系统性地评估了EEG基础模型内部表征的可靠性和可解释性，揭示了关键表征失败模式，并为临床可信任的模型干预提供了生理层面的解释途径。

Abstract: EEG foundation models achieve state-of-the-art clinical performance, yet the internal computations driving their predictions remain opaque: a barrier to clinical trust. We apply TopK Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) across three architecturally distinct EEG transformers: SleepFM, REVE, and LaBraM to extract sparse feature dictionaries from their embeddings. By grounding these features in a clinical taxonomy (abnormality, age, sex, and medication), we benchmark monosemanticity and entanglement across architectures. A single hyperparameter procedure, driven by an intrinsic dictionary health audit, transfers robustly across all three architectures. Via concept steering, we introduce a "target vs. off-target" probe area metric to quantify steering selectivity and reveal three operational regimes: selectively steerable, encoded but entangled, and non-encoded. This framework exposes critical representational failures: "wrecking-ball" interventions that collapse global model performance, and clinical entanglements, such as age-pathology confounding, where it is impossible to suppress one concept without corrupting the other. Finally, a spectral decoder maps these interventions back to the amplitude spectrum, translating latent manipulations into physiologically interpretable frequency signatures, such as pathological slow-wave suppression and $α$-band restoration.

</details>


### [19] [Rethinking Molecular OOD Generalization via Target-Aware Source Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13932)
*Zhuohao Lin,Kun Li,Jiameng Chen,Jiajun Yu,Duanhua Cao,Yizhen Zheng,Wenbin Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出SCOPE-BENCH基准测试和POMA框架，分别用于评估和提升分子性质在极端分布外场景下的预测性能。SCOPE-BENCH通过显式物理化学描述符空间的聚类级划分，揭示现有3D分子模型预测误差飙升可达8倍；POMA则通过强化学习策略自适应选择最优源域子集，结合宏观拓扑与微观药效团双尺度域适应，实现平均绝对误差降低6.2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前分子性质预测在极端分布外场景下存在两大问题：一是现有骨架划分方案无法消除微观语义重叠，使模型通过捷径学习高估外推能力；二是传统域适应范式在极端结构偏移下盲目对齐异质源库会注入拓扑噪声并引发负迁移。

Method: 1) SCOPE-BENCH：基于显式物理化学描述符空间的聚类级划分构建基准测试；2) POMA：设计检索-组合-适应三阶段知识迁移框架，先识别与无标签目标结构接近的有标签源骨架作为代理目标，再通过强化学习策略从指数级候选池中自适应选择最优源子集，最后在宏观拓扑与微观药效团两个尺度上进行域适应。

Result: 在SCOPE-BENCH上，最先进的3D分子模型预测误差飙升最高8.0倍，平均5.9倍；POMA在不同骨干架构上实现平均绝对误差降低最高11.2%，平均相对改进6.2%。

Conclusion: SCOPE-BENCH有效暴露了现有模型在极端OOD场景下的真实外推能力不足，POMA通过结构化知识迁移显著提升了分子性质预测的鲁棒性，为AI药物发现中的极端分布外泛化问题提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Robust prediction of molecular properties under extreme out-of-distribution (OOD) scenarios is a pivotal bottleneck in AI-driven drug discovery. Current scaffold-splitting protocols fail to obstruct microscopic semantic overlap, predisposing models to shortcut learning and overestimating their true extrapolation capability; meanwhile, conventional domain adaptation paradigms suffer under extreme structural shifts, as blindly aligning heterogeneous source libraries injects topological noise and triggers negative transfer. To address these two challenges, scaffold-cluster out-of-distribution performance evaluation benchmark (SCOPE-BENCH), a benchmark built on cluster-level partitioning in an explicit physicochemical descriptor space, is proposed alongside policy optimization for multi-source adaptation (POMA), a framework that formulates knowledge transfer as a retrieve-compose-adapt pipeline: labeled source scaffolds structurally close to the unlabeled target are first identified as proxy targets; a reinforcement learning policy then adaptively selects the optimal source subset from an exponentially large candidate pool; and dual-scale domain adaptation is finally performed at macroscopic topological and microscopic pharmacophore scales. Evaluations show that prediction errors of state-of-the-art 3D molecular models surge by up to 8.0x on SCOPE-BENCH with a mean of 5.9x, while POMA achieves up to an 11.2% reduction in mean absolute error with an average relative improvement of 6.2% across diverse backbone architectures. Code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/Molecular-OOD-Code-73F6.

### [20] [Unsupervised learning of acquisition variability in structural connectomes via hybrid latent space modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13933)
*Gaurav Rudravaram,Lianrui Zuo,Karthik Ramadass,Elyssa McMaster,Jongyeon Yoon,Aravind R. Krishnan,Adam M. Saunders,Chenyu Gao,Nancy R. Newlin,Praitayini Kanakaraj,Lori L. Beason Held,Murat Bilgel,Laura A. Barquero,Micah DArchangel,Tin Q. Nguyen,Laurie B. Cutting,Derek Archer,Timothy J. Hohman,Daniel C. Moyer,Bennett A. Landman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需人工调节的无监督框架Joint-VAE，通过架构退火（architectural annealing）技术在编码器输出后自适应平衡离散与连续潜变量，从而在结构连接组分析中分离采集差异（站点、扫描仪、协议）与生物变异。在N=7,416个dMRI结构连接组数据集上，该方法在捕获采集相关变异方面（ARI=0.53, p<0.05）优于标准VAE、PCA+k-means及基于损失退火的混合模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: dMRI数据中跨站点、扫描仪和协议的采集差异会引入变异性，干扰结构连接组分析。现有方法（如标准降维）将所有变异建模为连续，导致采集效应被吸收进连续潜空间；而混合潜空间模型虽引入离散分量，但需要手动调节容量来控制离散分量捕获意图的变异性。本文旨在消除这种手动调节需求。

Method: 提出Joint-VAE框架，核心创新是架构退火（architectural annealing）：在编码器输出后、解码器之前对编码结果进行退火处理，使模型在训练过程中自适应地平衡离散与连续潜变量，无需手动调节离散分量的容量。模型在混合连续-离散潜空间中联合建模平滑结构和类别结构。

Result: 在N=7,416个dMRI结构连接组数据集（年龄2-102岁，来自13项研究、25种采集参数组合）上，Joint-VAE在站点分类任务上达到ARI=0.53（p<0.05），显著优于标准VAE、PCA+k-means聚类以及仅通过损失函数退火的混合模型。

Conclusion: 基于架构退火的混合连续-离散潜空间模型（Joint-VAE）能够无监督地有效捕获dMRI中的采集变异性，通过联合建模平滑与类别结构，恢复出与扫描仪和协议差异对齐的聚类，为分离采集效应与生物变异提供了有用机制。

Abstract: Acquisition differences across sites, scanners, and protocols in dMRI introduce variability that complicates structural connectome analysis. This motivates deep learning models that can represent high-dimensional connectomes in a low-dimensional space while explicitly separating acquisition-related effects from biological variation. Conventional dimensionality reduction methods model all variance as continuous, so acquisition effects often get absorbed into a continuous latent space. Recent hybrid latent-space models combine discrete and continuous components to address this, but typically require manual capacity tuning to ensure the discrete component captures the intended variability. We introduce an unsupervised framework that removes this manual tuning by architecturally annealing encoder outputs before decoding, allowing the model to adaptively balance discrete and continuous latent variables during training. To evaluate it, we curated a dataset of N=7,416 structural connectomes derived from dMRI, spanning ages 2 to 102 and 13 studies with 25 unique acquisition-parameter combinations. Of these, 5,900 are cognitively unimpaired, 877 have mild cognitive impairment (MCI), and 639 have Alzheimer's disease (AD). We compare against a standard VAE, PCA with k-means clustering, and hybrid models that anneal only through the loss function. Our architectural annealing produces stronger site learning (ARI=0.53, p<0.05) than these baselines. Results show that a hybrid continuous-discrete latent space, with architectural rather than loss-based annealing, provides a useful unsupervised mechanism for capturing acquisition variability in dMRI: by jointly modeling smooth and categorical structure, the Joint-VAE recovers clusters aligned with scanner and protocol differences.

*Saba Ahmadi,Prasanna Parthasarathi,Yufei Cui*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TraFL提出轨迹流平衡目标，解决扩散语言模型后训练中因奖励驱动更新导致的轨迹锁定问题（过度集中概率质量于少数去噪路径），通过奖励倾斜目标分布和参考模型锚定，在数学推理和代码生成任务中唯一在所有基准长度设置下优于基模型的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散语言模型后训练方法大多采用奖励最大化目标，但存在轨迹锁定问题：奖励驱动的更新使概率质量过度集中于少数去噪路径，在重复采样时降低正确解的覆盖范围。

Method: 提出TraFL（Trajectory Flow baLancing），使用轨迹平衡目标将策略训练向奖励倾斜的目标分布，并锚定到冻结的参考模型；通过扩散兼容的序列级替代目标和学习的提示相关归一化实现实用化。

Result: 在数学推理和代码生成基准上，TraFL是唯一在所有基准长度设置下优于基模型的后训练方法，且优势随采样预算增加而持续；在Minerva Math和LiveCodeBench所有难度分割上保持领先。

Conclusion: TraFL通过轨迹平衡目标有效缓解了扩散语言模型后训练中的轨迹锁定问题，实现了更稳健且可扩展的性能提升。

Abstract: Diffusion language models are a promising alternative to autoregressive models, yet post-training methods for them largely adapt reward-maximizing objectives. We identify a central failure mode in this setting we call trajectory locking: sampled reward-driven updates over-concentrate probability mass onto a narrow set of denoising paths, reducing coverage of alternative correct solutions under repeated sampling. To address this, we propose TraFL (Trajectory Flow baLancing), a trajectory-balance objective that trains the policy toward a reward-tilted target distribution anchored to a frozen reference model. We make this practical for diffusion language models with a diffusion-compatible sequence-level surrogate and a learned prompt-dependent normalization. Across mathematical reasoning and code generation benchmarks, TraFL is the only evaluated post-training method that improves over the base model in every benchmark-length setting, with gains that persist as the sampling budget increases. The improvements transfer to held-out evaluations: TraFL stays above the base model on Minerva Math and is the strongest method on every LiveCodeBench difficulty split.

Method: 基于Sherpa.ai联邦学习平台构建框架，使各节点在不交换私有数据的情况下联合微调共享LLM。采用LoRA、QLoRA和IA3三种参数高效微调策略，在医疗（MedQA、MedMCQA）和金融（FPB、FiQA-SA）四个数据集上进行评估，模拟非IID设置以反映真实机构数据异质性。

Abstract: The recent success of large language models (LLMs) has been largely driven by vast public datasets. However, the next frontier for LLM development lies beyond public data. Much of the world's most valuable information is private, especially in highly regulated sectors such as healthcare and finance, where data include patient histories or customer communications. Unlocking this data could represent a major leap forward, enabling LLMs with deeper domain expertise and stronger real-world utility. Yet, these data cannot be shared because they are distributed across institutions and constrained by privacy, regulatory, and organizational barriers. Moreover, institutional datasets are typically non-independent and identically distributed (non-IID), differing across sites in population characteristics, data modalities, documentation patterns, and task-specific label distributions.
  In this paper, we demonstrate a practical approach to unlocking private and distributed institutional data for LLM adaptation through federated collaboration across data silos. Built on the Sherpa.ai Federated Learning platform, our framework enables nodes to jointly fine-tune a shared LLM without exchanging private data. We evaluate this approach through a cross-domain benchmark in healthcare and finance, using four closed-ended question answering and classification datasets: MedQA, MedMCQA, FPB, and FiQA-SA. We compare three parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) strategies-LoRA, QLoRA, and IA3-across pretrained backbones under non-IID settings reflecting institutional data heterogeneity. Our results show that federated fine-tuning performs close to centralized training and outperforms isolated single-institution learning. From a Green AI perspective, QLoRA and IA3 improve efficiency with limited accuracy degradation, supporting federated PEFT as a viable approach for adapting LLMs where data cannot be shared.

### [23] [EvolveMem:Self-Evolving Memory Architecture via AutoResearch for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13941)
*Jiaqi Liu,Xinyu Ye,Peng Xia,Zeyu Zheng,Cihang Xie,Mingyu Ding,Huaxiu Yao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EvolveMem提出了一种自进化记忆架构，不仅让存储内容演化，还让检索机制（评分函数、融合策略、答案生成策略）也随之自适应演化。通过LLM驱动的诊断模块和闭环自演化流程，在LoCoMo和MemBench上分别超越最强基线25.7%和18.9%，且进化出的配置可跨基准正向迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体记忆系统将检索基础设施视为固定不变的，仅存储内容会演化，而评分函数、融合策略和答案生成策略在部署后冻结。真正的自适应记忆需要存储知识和检索机制两个层面的共同演化。

Method: EvolveMem将完整检索配置暴露为结构化动作空间，由LLM驱动的诊断模块读取失败日志、识别根本原因并提出配置调整建议；采用带自动回滚（revert-on-regression）和停滞探索（explore-on-stagnation）保护的元分析器执行调整，形成闭环自进化流程（AutoResearch）。

Result: 在LoCoMo上超越最强基线25.7%，相对最小基线提升78.0%；在MemBench上超越最强基线18.9%。进化出的配置可跨基准正向迁移，表明学到了通用检索原理而非基准特定启发式。

Conclusion: EvolveMem通过让检索机制与存储内容共同演化，实现了真正的自适应记忆，其自进化过程能发现原始动作空间中不存在的新配置维度，且具有跨基准泛化能力。

Abstract: Long-term memory is essential for LLM agents that operate across multiple sessions, yet existing memory systems treat retrieval infrastructure as fixed: stored content evolves while scoring functions, fusion strategies, and answer-generation policies remain frozen at deployment. We argue that truly adaptive memory requires co-evolution at two levels: the stored knowledge and the retrieval mechanism that queries it. We present EvolveMem, a self-evolving memory architecture that exposes its full retrieval configuration as a structured action space optimized by an LLM-powered diagnosis module. In each evolution round, the module reads per-question failure logs, identifies root causes, and proposes targeted configuration adjustments; a guarded meta-analyzer applies them with automatic revert-on-regression and explore-on-stagnation safeguards. This closed-loop self-evolution realizes an AutoResearch process: the system autonomously conducts iterative research cycles on its own architecture, replacing manual configuration tuning. Starting from a minimal baseline, the process converges autonomously, discovering effective retrieval strategies including entirely new configuration dimensions not present in the original action space. On LoCoMo, EvolveMem outperforms the strongest baseline by 25.7% relative and achieves a 78.0% relative improvement over the minimal baseline. On MemBench, EvolveMem exceeds the strongest baseline by 18.9% relative. Evolved configurations transfer across benchmarks with positive rather than catastrophic transfer, indicating that the self-evolution process captures universal retrieval principles rather than benchmark-specific heuristics. Code is available at https://github.com/aiming-lab/SimpleMem.

### [24] [EMA: Efficient Model Adaptation for Learning-based Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13942)
*Daiyang Yu,Xinyu Chen,Yihan Zhang,Yan Liang,Yaqi Qiao,Fan Lai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EMA是首个支持学习型系统在异构、动态环境中自适应演进的模型适配系统，通过状态变换器降低训练成本，通过优先标记高效用数据降低标记成本，在8个代表性系统上实现14.9-42.4%的训练成本降低和6.9-31.3%的系统性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于学习的系统在网络等动态异构环境中缺乏有效的自适应机制，导致模型训练成本高、数据收集量大、系统性能下降且响应缓慢。

Method: 采用系统驱动、数据为中心的方法：(1) 提出状态变换器（State Transformers），将新环境的输入状态对齐到先前相似状态，实现模型的热启动自适应；(2) 通过优先标记高效用数据，平衡训练成本与标记成本之间的权衡。

Result: 在8个代表性学习型系统上，EMA将适配成本（如GPU训练时间）降低14.9-42.4%，同时将系统性能（如网络吞吐量）提升6.9-31.3%。

Conclusion: EMA有效解决了学习型系统在动态环境下的自适应部署难题，以最小操作开销实现了显著的成本降低和性能提升。

Abstract: Machine learning (ML) is increasingly applied to optimize system performance in tasks such as resource management and network simulation. Unlike traditional ML tasks (e.g., image classification), networked systems often operate in heterogeneous, long-running, and dynamic environment states, where input conditions (e.g., network loads) and operational objectives can shift over time and across settings. Existing learning-based systems offer little support for adaptation, resulting in costly model training, extensive data collection, degraded system performance, and slow responsiveness.
  This paper presents EMA, the first model adaptation system supporting learning-based systems to adapt to evolving environments with minimal operational overhead. EMA takes a system-driven, data-centric approach that accommodates diverse system and model designs while addressing two key deployment challenges. First, it reduces expensive model training by introducing state transformers that align the input state of a new environment with previously similar states, allowing models to warm-start adaptation. Second, it addresses the often-overlooked yet costly process of data labeling--collecting ground truth for exploring and training on various system decisions--by prioritizing labeling high-utility data while balancing the tradeoff between training and labeling cost. Evaluations on eight representative learning-based systems show that EMA reduces adaptation costs (e.g., GPU training time) by 14.9-42.4% while improving system performance (e.g., network throughput) by 6.9-31.3%.

### [25] [A Unified Geometric Framework for Weighted Contrastive Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13943)
*Raphael Vock,Edouard Duchesnay,Benoit Dufumier*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过将加权InfoNCE目标解释为距离几何问题，揭示了对比学习嵌入的几何结构：在监督分类中，SupCon在类别不平衡时产生非均匀类间相似度，而Soft SupCon保持正则单纯形；在连续标签场景中，y-Aware CL的标签权重与球形潜在相似度存在几何不匹配，导致无法达到熵最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对比学习旨在通过反映相似性图的表示来保持样本间的关系结构，但所得嵌入的几何结构尚不明确。本文旨在从距离几何视角揭示加权对比学习目标的几何特性。

Method: 将加权InfoNCE目标重新解释为距离几何问题（DGP），通过理论分析推导监督和弱监督设置下最优嵌入的精确表征。

Result: 1) 监督SupCon和Soft SupCon将同类样本坍缩到单一原型；2) 平衡SupCon恢复正则单纯形，但类别不平衡导致非均匀类间相似度；3) Soft SupCon无论类别平衡与否均保持正则单纯形；4) y-Aware CL在连续标签下仅当标签位于超球面时才能达到熵最优；5) 几何一致的选择（如欧几里得-欧几里得加权或X-CLR）具有唯一最优嵌入。

Conclusion: 加权方案的选择决定了对比学习是否几何可实现、退化或不一致，为设计对比学习目标提供了原则性框架。

Abstract: Contrastive learning (CL) aims to preserve relational structure between samples by learning representations that reflect a similarity graph. Yet, the geometry of the resulting embeddings remains poorly understood. Here we show that weighted InfoNCE objectives can be interpreted as Distance Geometry Problems, where the weighting scheme specifies the target geometry to be realized by the representation. This viewpoint yields exact characterizations of the optimal embeddings for several supervised and weakly supervised objectives. In supervised classification, both SupCon and Soft SupCon (a dense relaxation of it where pairs from distinct classes have small non-zero similarity) collapse samples within each class to a single prototype. However, while balanced SupCon recovers the classical regular simplex geometry, class imbalance breaks this symmetry: SupCon induces non-uniform inter-class similarities depending on class sizes, whereas Soft SupCon preserves a regular simplex geometry regardless of class imbalance. In continuous-label settings, our framework reveals a different failure mode: y-Aware CL generally cannot attain its entropic optimum unless the labels lie on a hypersphere, exposing a mismatch between Euclidean label weights and spherical latent similarity. By contrast, geometrically consistent choices such as Euclidean-Euclidean weighting or X-CLR admit unique optimal embeddings. Our results show that the choice of weighting scheme determines whether contrastive learning is geometrically realizable, degenerate, or inconsistent, providing a principled framework for designing contrastive objectives.

</details>

*Darius A. Faroughy,Sofia Palacios Schweitzer,Ian Pang,Siddharth Mishra-Sharma,David Shih*

Abstract: Autonomous language-model agents are increasingly evaluated on long-horizon tool-use tasks, but existing benchmarks rarely capture the complexity and nuance of real scientific work. To address this gap, we introduce Collider-Bench, a benchmark for evaluating whether LLM agents can reproduce experimental analyses from the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) using only public papers and open scientific software. Such analyses are often difficult to reproduce because the public toolchain only approximates the software used internally by the experimental collaborations, while the published papers inevitably omit implementation details needed for a faithful reconstruction. Agents must therefore rely on physical reasoning, domain knowledge, and trial-and-error to fill these gaps. Each task requires the agent to turn a published analysis into an executable simulation-and-selection pipeline and submit predicted collision event yields in specified signal regions. These predictions are evaluated with standard histogram metrics that provide continuous fidelity scores without a hand-written rubric. We also report the computational cost incurred by each agent per task. Finally, we evaluate the codebase and full session trace using an LLM judge to catch qualitative failure modes such as fabrications, hallucinations and duplications. We release an initial set of tasks drawn from LHC searches, together with a containerized sandbox and event simulation tools. We evaluate across a capability ladder of general purpose coding agents. Our results show that on average no agent reliably beats the physicist-in-the-loop solution.

*Léo Grinsztajn,Klemens Flöge,Oscar Key,Felix Birkel,Philipp Jund,Brendan Roof,Mihir Manium,Shi Bin,Hoo,Magnus Bühler,Anurag Garg,Dominik Safaric,Jake Robertson,Benjamin Jäger,Simone Alessi,Adrian Hayler,Vladyslav Moroshan,Lennart Purucker,Philipp Singer,Alan Arazi,Julien Siems,Jan Hendrik Metzen,Georg Grab,Nick Erickson,Siyuan Guo,Eliott Kalfon,Simon Bing,David Salinas,Clara Cornu,Lilly Charlotte Wehrhahn,Diana Kriuchkova,Kursat Kaya,Lydia Sidhoum,Marie Salmon,Jerry Chen,Madelon Hulsebos,Yann LeCun,Samuel Müller,Bernhard Schölkopf,Sauraj Gambhir,Noah Hollmann,Frank Hutter*

<details>

Method: 完全使用先验分布生成的合成数据预训练；引入测试时计算扩展（Test-time Compute Scaling）；采用缩减KV缓存和行分块（row-chunking）技术，实现在单张H100上扩展到100万行且推理速度快；提供TabPFN-3-Plus (Thinking) API版本利用测试时计算提升性能。

Result: 在TabArena标准基准上，前向传播即超越所有调优和集成基线，在速度/性能前沿上帕累托占优；在多样数据集上，多类别数据集排名第一，在百万行/200特征数据集上击败8小时调优的GBDT基线；TabPFN-3-Plus在TabArena上领先非TabPFN模型超200 Elo，最大数据子集上达420 Elo；比AutoGluon 1.5 extreme快10倍且性能更优；在RelBenchV1上达到新SOTA，在TabSTAR上达SOTA；TabPFN-TS-3在fev-bench时间序列基准上排名第二；SHAP值计算快120倍；比TabPFN-2.5快20倍。

Conclusion: TabPFN-3显著推进了表格预测的前沿，在多个模态（表格、时间序列、关系数据、表格-文本）上达到SOTA，同时大幅提升速度，证明了纯粹基于合成数据预训练的表格基础模型能够以更快的速度全面超越传统调优方法。

Abstract: Tabular data underpins most high-value prediction problems in science and industry, and TabPFN has driven the foundation model revolution for this modality. Designed with feedback from our users, TabPFN-3 builds on this foundation to scale state-of-the-art performance to datasets with 1M training rows and substantially reduce training and inference time. Pretrained exclusively on synthetic data from our prior, TabPFN-3 dramatically pushes the frontier of tabular prediction and brings substantial gains on time series, relational, and tabular-text data. On the standard tabular benchmark TabArena, a forward pass of TabPFN-3 outperforms all other models, including tuned and ensembled baselines, by a significant margin, and pareto-dominates the speed/performance frontier. On more diverse datasets, TabPFN-3 ranks first on datasets with many classes, and beats 8-hour-tuned gradient-boosted-tree baselines on datasets up to 1M training rows and 200 features. TabPFN-3 introduces test-time compute scaling to tabular foundation models. Our API offering TabPFN-3-Plus (Thinking) exploits this to beat all non-TabPFN models by over 200 Elo on TabArena, rising to 420 Elo on the largest data subset, and outperforms AutoGluon 1.5 extreme while being 10x faster, without using LLMs, real data, internet search or any other model besides TabPFN. TabPFN-3 extends the capabilities of our models, enabling SOTA prediction on relational data (new SOTA foundation model on RelBenchV1) and tabular-text data (SOTA on TabSTAR via TabPFN-3-Plus); and improves existing integrations: a specialized checkpoint, TabPFN-TS-3, ranks 2nd on the time-series benchmark fev-bench, and SHAP-value computation is up to 120x faster. TabPFN-3 achieves this performance while being up to 20x faster than TabPFN-2.5. In addition, a reduced KV cache and row-chunking scale to 1M rows on one H100 with fast inference speed.

### [30] [Neural Fields for NV-Center Inverse Sensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13988)
*Zhixuan Zhao,Tao Zhong,Yixun Hu,Nathalie P. de Leon,Christine Allen-Blanchette*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对NV量子传感中的逆问题，指出标量/相干前向近似会导致中心坍缩失效模式，提出NeTMY——一种无摊销坐标神经场耦合可微NV前向模型的方法，结合退火位置编码、多尺度优化、稀疏门控和谱保真度损失，在修正算子生成的稀疏合成重建中取得最佳性能，并通过机制实验揭示其参数化平滑并重新分布梯度更新，缓解中心坍缩病理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统逆问题方法（手工正则化器或监督网络）在面临非线性、谱耦合且物理敏感的量子传感前向模型时容易失效，尤其是NV色心磁噪声传感中，稀疏自旋源的重建受到前向近似误差和自由密度优化中的中心坍缩问题的困扰。

Method: 提出NeTMY方法：无摊销坐标神经场，耦合可微NV前向模型；采用退火位置编码、多尺度优化、稀疏门控机制和谱保真度损失函数进行端到端优化。

Result: 在修正的张量幂和偶极算子生成的稀疏合成重建基准测试中，NeTMY在定位指标和分布指标上均取得最佳性能；机制实验表明NeTMY不直接执行原始密度空间梯度，其参数化平滑并重新分布梯度更新，有效缓解了中心坍缩病理。

Abstract: Inverse problems in scientific sensing are often solved with either hand-designed regularizers or supervised networks trained on simulated labels, yet both can fail when the forward model is nonlinear, spectrally coupled, and physically delicate. We study this issue for noise sensing based on nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers in diamond, where a quantum sensor measures magnetic-noise spectra generated by sparse spin sources. We show that replacing a common scalar/coherent forward approximation with a tensor power-summed dipolar operator changes the inverse landscape and exposes a center-collapse failure mode in free-density optimization. We propose NeTMY, an amortization-free coordinate neural field coupled to the differentiable NV forward model, with annealed positional encoding, multiscale optimization, sparsity/gating, and spectrum-fidelity losses. Across sparse synthetic reconstructions generated by the corrected operator, NeTMY achieves the best localization and distributional metrics in the tested benchmark. Mechanism experiments show that NeTMY does not directly execute the raw density-space gradient; its parameterization smooths and redistributes updates, mitigating the center-collapse pathology. These results position NV quantum sensing as a useful testbed for physics-faithful neural inverse problems.

### [31] [HodgeCover: Higher-Order Topological Coverage Drives Compression of Sparse Mixture-of-Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13997)
*Tao Zhong,Dongzhe Zheng,Christine Allen-Blanchette*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现稀疏MoE层中三个两两兼容的专家可能形成不可约的合并循环，该结构障碍对应2-复形上的调和核；提出HodgeCover方法贪婪覆盖调和关键边和三元组关键三角面，结合混合剪枝策略，在激进压缩下达到最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无训练压缩方法使用两两专家间的兼容性分数来指导合并，但忽略了三元组及以上专家组合可能形成不可约循环（即两两可合并但三者不可同时合并）的结构性障碍，导致压缩质量受限。

Method: 将专家视为顶点、KL散度合并障碍视为边、三元组合并障碍视为面，构建2-复形；通过Hodge分解将边信号分解，分离出调和核；提出HodgeCover算法，贪婪覆盖调和关键边和三元组关键三角面；混合版本结合权重剪枝。

Conclusion: 暴露MoE结构的调和核改变了激进压缩场景下的最优压缩策略，HodgeCover在无训练压缩家族中具有独特优势。

Abstract: Sparse Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) layers route tokens through a handful of experts, and learning-free compression of these layers reduces inference cost without retraining. A subtle obstruction blocks every existing compressor in this family: three experts can each be pairwise compatible yet form an irreducible cycle when merged together, so any score that ranks experts on pairwise signals is structurally blind to which triples are jointly mergeable. We show the obstruction is a precise mathematical object, the harmonic kernel of the simplicial Laplacian on a 2-complex whose vertices are experts, whose edges carry KL merge barriers, and whose faces carry triplet barriers; Hodge-decomposing the edge-barrier signal isolates the kernel exactly. We turn the diagnostic into a selection objective: HodgeCover greedily covers the harmonic-critical edges and triplet-critical triangles, and a hybrid variant of HodgeCover pairs it with off-the-shelf weight pruning on survivors. On three open-weight Sparse MoE backbones under aggressive expert reduction, HodgeCover matches state-of-the-art learning-free baselines on the expert-reduction axis, leads on the aggressive-compression frontier of the hybrid axis, and uniquely balances retained mass across all four Hodge components. These results show that exposing the harmonic kernel of a learned MoE structure changes which compressor wins at the regime that matters most.

### [32] [Support Before Frequency in Discrete Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13999)
*Adrian Müller,Antoine Gonon,Zebang Shen,Ya-Ping Hsieh,Niao He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文证明了离散扩散模型（均匀和吸收/掩码）在去噪过程中存在层次结构：最终步骤中，每个单令牌反向编辑被分解为“支持尺度”（是否向数据支持移动，如语法有效句子）和“频率系数”（相同尺度内的相对概率）。恢复有效性结构只需学习反向概率的量级，而恢复数据频率需要系数级估计。实验验证了支持定位早于频率排序，且均匀与吸收扩散的分离机制不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管离散扩散模型在语言建模中表现越来越有竞争力，但其去噪目标如何组织学习过程仍不清晰。虽然这些目标针对完整数据分布，但本文旨在揭示精确反向过程中粗粒度支持信息与细粒度频率信息之间的层次关系。

Method: 理论证明：在小噪声区域（最终去噪步骤），均匀扩散和吸收（掩码）扩散的单令牌反向编辑分解为领先尺度（是否向数据支持移动）和更细的系数（相同尺度内的相对概率）。通过分析两种扩散机制的不同分离特性，并通过实验验证。

Result: 均匀扩散呈现三分法：有效性改进、维持和恶化编辑；吸收扩散的主导质量落在有效性改进移动上。实验表明：支持定位先于频率排序出现，均匀与吸收扩散的对比符合预测的速率分离。

Conclusion: 离散扩散模型先学习数据支持（如语法合法性），后学习数据频率（如词汇分布概率）。这解释了为什么模型能先学会生成有效句子，然后再精细调整词汇选择概率。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion models are increasingly competitive for language modeling, yet it remains unclear how their denoising objectives organize learning. Although these objectives target the full data distribution, we show that the exact reverse process induces a hierarchy between coarse support information and finer frequency information. For uniform and absorbing (a.k.a. masking) diffusion, we prove that, in the small-noise regime of the final denoising steps, each single-token reverse edit decomposes into a leading scale, determined by whether it moves toward the data support (e.g., grammatically valid sentences), and a finer coefficient, determining relative probabilities within the same scale. Thus, recovering validity structure only requires learning the correct order of magnitude of reverse probabilities, whereas recovering data frequencies requires coefficient-level estimation. The separation is mechanism-dependent: uniform diffusion exhibits a trichotomy into validity-improving, validity-preserving, and validity-worsening edits, while absorbing diffusion places its leading-order mass on validity-improving moves. Experiments on a masked language diffusion model and synthetic regular-language tasks support these predictions: support-localization emerges earlier than within-support frequency ranking, and the contrast between uniform and absorbing diffusion matches the predicted rate separation. Together, our results suggest that discrete diffusion models learn data support before data frequencies.

</details>

### [34] [Policy Optimization in Hybrid Discrete-Continuous Action Spaces via Mixed Gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14297)
*Matias Alvo,Daniel Russo,Yash Kanoria*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出混合策略优化（HPO），一种针对混合离散-连续动作空间的强化学习方法，通过在平滑部分使用路径梯度、非平滑部分使用得分函数梯度的混合无偏梯度估计器，在库存控制和切换线性二次型调节器问题上显著优于PPO。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法面临两难：模型无关策略梯度方法依赖得分函数估计器，在高维连续动作空间中存在严重的信用分配问题，梯度质量差；而可微模拟器虽可通过反向传播缓解该问题，但离散动作或非平滑动力学会导致有偏或无效的梯度。需要一种能兼顾两者的方法。

Method: 提出HPO算法，核心是混合梯度估计器：在动力学平滑的位置使用路径梯度（通过模拟器反向传播），在非平滑或离散决策处使用得分函数梯度，并保持无偏性。此外，将存在动作不连续性的问题重新表述为混合形式以扩大适用范围，并分析了混合梯度的交叉项结构。

Result: 在库存控制和切换线性二次型调节器问题上，HPO显著优于PPO，且随着连续动作维度增加，性能差距进一步扩大。理论上证明了混合梯度中的交叉项（连续动作影响未来离散决策的项）在离散最优响应附近可忽略，从而允许连续和离散组件近似解耦更新，降低方差。

Conclusion: HPO通过混合梯度估计器有效结合了可微模拟器的精度和策略梯度的通用性，在混合离散-连续动作空间问题中取得了显著性能提升，且理论分析揭示了其在高维和接近最优时的高效性。

Abstract: We study reinforcement learning in hybrid discrete-continuous action spaces, such as settings where the discrete component selects a regime (or index) and the continuous component optimizes within it -- a structure common in robotics, control, and operations problems. Standard model-free policy gradient methods rely on score-function (SF) estimators and suffer from severe credit-assignment issues in high-dimensional settings, leading to poor gradient quality. On the other hand, differentiable simulation largely sidesteps these issues by backpropagating through a simulator, but the presence of discrete actions or non-smooth dynamics yields biased or uninformative gradients. To address this, we propose Hybrid Policy Optimization (HPO), which backpropagates through the simulator wherever smoothness permits, using a mixed gradient estimator that combines pathwise and SF gradients while maintaining unbiasedness. We also show how problems with action discontinuities can be reformulated in hybrid form, further broadening its applicability. Empirically, HPO substantially outperforms PPO on inventory control and switched linear-quadratic regulator problems, with performance gaps increasing as the continuous action dimension grows. Finally, we characterize the structure of the mixed gradient, showing that its cross term -- which captures how continuous actions influence future discrete decisions -- becomes negligible near a discrete best response, thereby enabling approximate decentralized updates of the continuous and discrete components and reducing variance near optimality. All resources are available at github.com/MatiasAlvo/hybrid-rl.

</details>

To bridge this gap, we propose Robust Representation via Redundancy Reduction (R2R2), a regularization method within SPL. We theoretically identify that standard zero-centering conflicts with SPL's spectral properties and design a non-centered objective accordingly. We verify R2R2 on SPL-native algorithms like TD7. Furthermore, to demonstrate its orthogonality to prior advancements, we extend the state-of-the-art SimbaV2, which originally lacks SPL, by integrating a tailored SPL module, termed SimbaV2-SPL. Experiments across 11 continuous control tasks confirm that R2R2 effectively mitigates overfitting; specifically, at a UTD ratio of 20, it improves TD7 by ~22% and provides additional gains on top of SimbaV2-SPL, which itself establishes a new state-of-the-art. ### [38] [Self-Pruned Key-Value Attention: Learning When to Write by Predicting Future Utility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14037)
*Gergely Szilvasy,Manuel Faysse,Maria Lomeli,Matthijs Douze,Pierre-Emmanuel Mazaré,Loïc Cabannes,Wen-tau Yih,Hervé Jégou*

TL;DR: SP-KV是一种动态剪枝的键值注意力机制，通过预测每个KV对的未来效用，在保留局部窗口的同时选择性保留高效用KV用于全局注意力，从而实现3-10倍的KV缓存压缩，显著提升内存效率和解码速度，且几乎不损失性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现代测试时计算和智能体范式下，语言模型处理的序列越来越长，Transformer架构中的KV缓存内存占用和带宽成为高效文本生成的主要瓶颈。

Method: 提出Self-Pruned Key-Value Attention (SP-KV)，包含一个轻量级效用预测器为每个KV对打分；近期KV始终通过局部窗口可用，而较旧的KV仅当预测效用超过阈值时才写入缓存并用于全局注意力；LLM与效用预测器通过下一token预测损失进行端到端联合训练，从预训练LLM检查点适配而来。

Result: SP-KV实现动态稀疏化，通常将KV缓存大小压缩3-10倍，较长序列压缩率更高；在验证损失和下游任务性能上几乎无退化，显著改善内存使用和解码速度；揭示了结构化的逐层和逐头稀疏模式。

Conclusion: SP-KV不仅是一种有效的KV缓存缩减机制，其揭示的稀疏模式还可用于指导混合局部-全局注意力架构的设计。

Abstract: Under modern test-time compute and agentic paradigms, language models process ever-longer sequences. Efficient text generation with transformer architectures is increasingly constrained by the Key-Value cache memory footprint and bandwidth. To address this limitation, we introduce Self-Pruned Key-Value Attention (SP-KV), a mechanism designed to predict future KV utility in order to reduce the size of the long-term KV cache. This strategy operates at a fine granularity: a lightweight utility predictor scores each key-value pair, and while recent KVs are always available via a local window, older pairs are written in the cache and used in global attention only if their predicted utility surpasses a given threshold. The LLM and the utility predictor are trained jointly end-to-end exclusively through next-token prediction loss, and are adapted from pretrained LLM checkpoints.
  Rather than enforcing a fixed compression ratio, SP-KV performs dynamic sparsification: the mechanism adapts to the input and typically reduces the KV cache size by a factor of $3$ to $10\times$, longer sequences often being more compressible. This leads to vast improvements in memory usage and decoding speed, with little to no degradation of validation loss nor performance on a broad set of downstream tasks. Beyond serving as an effective KV-cache reduction mechanism, our method reveals structured layer- and head-specific sparsity patterns that we can use to guide the design of hybrid local-global attention architectures.

Abstract: Deep learning methods based on backward stochastic differential equations (BSDEs) have emerged as competitive alternatives to physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) for solving high-dimensional partial differential equations (PDEs). By leveraging probabilistic representations, BSDE approaches can avoid the curse of dimensionality and often admit second-order-free training objectives that do not require explicit Hessian evaluations. It has recently been established that the commonly used Euler-Maruyama (EM) time discretization induces an intrinsic bias in BSDE training losses. While high-order schemes such as Heun can fully eliminate this bias, such schemes re-introduce second-order spatial derivatives and incur substantial computational overhead. ### [40] [How to Scale Mixture-of-Experts: From muP to the Maximally Scale-Stable Parameterization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14200)
*Leena Chennuru Vankadara,Moritz Haas,Luke Hayward,Sebastian Bordt,Alessandro Breccia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对混合专家模型（MoE）架构，分析了三种不同的缩放机制，发展了动力学平均场理论（DMFT）描述训练动力学，推导了满足μP参数化的唯一形式，发现μP无法可靠实现单调缩放改进和学习率迁移，进而提出了最大尺度稳定性（MSSP）的新参数化方法，实验验证MSSP在多种缩放机制下都能稳定恢复学习率迁移和单调性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管MoE架构在前沿大语言模型中广泛使用，但缺乏对超参数如何随网络宽度、专家宽度、专家数量、稀疏度和深度缩放的理论理解，现有实践缺乏原则性指导。

Method: 定义了三种缩放机制（共缩放、协同缩放、全比例缩放），为每种机制发展DMFT描述极限训练动力学，推导满足μP性质的唯一参数化方案，识别μP的病理学问题后提出MSSP原则并推导对应的参数化方案。

Result: μP无法可靠实现单调性能改进和学习率迁移；MSSP在所有缩放机制下都能稳定恢复学习率迁移和单调性能提升。

Conclusion: 结合已有深度缩放理论，MSSP提供了MoE架构在宽度、深度、专家宽度和专家数量方面的完整缩放处方。

Abstract: Recent frontier large language models predominantly rely on Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures. Despite empirical progress, there is still no principled understanding of how hyperparameters should scale with network width $N$, expert width $N_e$, number of experts $M$, sparsity $K$, and depth $L$ to ensure both stability and optimal performance at scale. We take a principled step toward resolving this gap by analyzing three different scaling regimes: (I) co-scaling $N\asymp N_e$, (II) co-scaling $N\asymp M\asymp K$, and (III) full proportional scaling of $N, N_e, M$, and $K$. For each regime, we develop a novel Dynamical Mean Field Theory (DMFT) description of the limiting training dynamics of MoEs that provides a formal foundation for our analysis. Within this framework, we derive the unique parameterization for SGD and Adam satisfying all maximal-update ($μ$) desiderata. We then show that the resulting $μ$P prescription does not reliably induce monotonic improvement with scale or robust learning-rate transfer. We trace these pathologies to scale-dependent observables in the aggregation dynamics, which motivates a refined set of desiderata that we term maximal scale stability. Guided by this principle, we derive a Maximally Scale-Stable Parameterization (MSSP) for both SGD and Adam in all three scaling regimes, and characterize the corresponding limiting dynamics - qualitatively distinct from the $μ$P limit - through a separate DMFT analysis. Experiments verify that MSSP robustly recovers learning rate transfer and monotonic improvement with scale across regimes. Combined with existing depth-scaling theory, these results provide a complete scaling prescription for MoE architectures as a function of width, depth, expert width, and number of experts.

### [41] [Reliability-Gated Source Anchoring for Continual Test-Time Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14063)
*Vikash Singh,Debargha Ganguly,Weicong Chen,Sabyasachi Sahoo,Sreehari Sankar,Biyao Zhang,Mohsen Harir,Shouren Wang,Osama Zafar,Christian Gagné,Vipin Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出RMemSafe，一种基于可靠性门控的持续测试时适应方法，通过检测源模型预测熵的异常升高来动态关闭源锚定机制，在源模型失效时切换到无源回退方案，有效解决了盲锚定问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的源锚定CTTA方法在源模型性能严重退化时（如CCC-Hard上ResNet-50仅1.3% top-1准确率）仍以固定强度施加源锚定，导致"盲锚定"失败模式。需要一种能感知源模型可靠性并自适应调整锚定强度的方法。

Method: RMemSafe是ROID的扩展，引入可靠性门控机制：使用冻结源模型的归一化预测熵作为源可靠性的指示器。当源后验接近均匀分布（高熵）时，门控关闭，消除源锚定和一致性过滤，目标函数退化为无源回退方案（ROID基础损失+边际校准）。

Result: 在9个匹配分割的持续污染单元格中，RMemSafe+ASR在8个上取得最低错误率，在所有9个上是最优的重置方法。相比ROID+ASR，ResNet-50提升1.05个百分点，ViT-B/16提升0.48个百分点。源退化扫描实验中，性能下降斜率比ROID+ASR浅1.13倍，验证了优雅退化特性。

Conclusion: 熵门控能够有效检测高熵源坍塌（而非置信度错误但低熵的源），其作用范围经过明确评估。RMemSafe在源模型不可靠时自动切换到无源回退方案，实现了对源模型可靠性变化的鲁棒适应。

Abstract: Continual test-time adaptation (CTTA) updates a pretrained model online on an unlabeled, non-stationary stream while anchoring it to a frozen source checkpoint. This anchor is useful only when the source remains reliable. On CCC-Hard, however, a ResNet-50 source falls to approximately $1.3\%$ top-$1$ accuracy, while existing source-anchored CTTA methods continue applying the same anchor strength. We call this failure mode blind anchoring and propose RMemSafe, a reliability-gated extension of ROID that uses the frozen source's normalized predictive entropy to attenuate all explicit source-coupled uses in the objective. When the source posterior approaches uniformity, the gate closes: the source anchor and agreement filter vanish, and the objective reduces to a source-agnostic fallback comprising ROID's base losses plus marginal calibration. Combined with ASR, RMemSafe achieves the lowest error on $8$ of $9$ matched-split continual-corruption cells and is the best reset-based method on all $9$, improving ROID+ASR by $1.05$~pp on ResNet-50 and $0.48$~pp on ViT-B/16. A controlled source-degradation sweep shows a $1.13{\times}$ shallower harm slope than ROID+ASR, consistent with the graceful-decay prediction. The entropy gate detects high-entropy source collapse, not confidently wrong low-entropy sources; this scope is explicitly evaluated and discussed.

</details>


### [42] [In-Context Learning for Data-Driven Censored Inventory Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14840)
*Sohom Mukherjee,Anh-Duy Pham,Richard Pibernik,Yunbei Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于上下文生成式后验采样（ICGPS）的库存控制方法，结合离线元训练的生成模型与在线自回归生成，有效处理决策依赖的右删失需求数据，理论证明了贝叶斯遗憾界，并通过ChronosFlow框架在实验中展现出对先验错配和分布偏移的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统参数化的汤普森采样方法在先验错配下表现脆弱，而离线插补方法无法直接迁移到在线学习场景。现有方法缺乏一种既能利用离线数据学习需求分布、又能在在线决策中灵活适应的统一框架。

Method: 提出ICGPS，结合离线元训练的生成模型与在线上下文自回归生成，通过学习潜在需求的完成（completion）来采取oracle动作。理论分析将ICGPS的贝叶斯遗憾分解为理想TS基准的遗憾加上一个依赖于补全错配的$\sqrt{T}$量级部署惩罚。在R-NV问题中，将删失反馈降维为带状凸优化反馈，证明次线性贝叶斯遗憾。实践中，使用ChronosFlow（冻结时间序列Transformer骨干+可训练条件归一化流头部）进行快速删失一致性采样。

Result: 理论证明了ICGPS的贝叶斯遗憾界；R-NV问题中获得次线性贝叶斯遗憾；实验表明ChronosFlow-ICGPS匹配正确指定的TS、优于myopic和UCB基线，对先验错配和分布偏移鲁棒，在真实SuperStore数据集上表现良好，尤其在强删失场景下。

Conclusion: ICGPS提供了一个即插即用的模板框架，可将离线学习能力迁移到在线决策问题中，在删失数据场景下具备理论保证和实际鲁棒性。

Abstract: We study inventory control with decision-dependent censoring, focusing on the censored or repeated newsvendor (R-NV), where each order quantity determines whether demand is fully observed or censored by sales. Existing approaches based on parametric Thompson sampling (TS) can be brittle under prior mismatch, while offline imputation methods need not transfer to online learning. Motivated by the predictive view of decision making, we combine these ideas by taking oracle actions on learned completions of latent demand. We propose in-context generative posterior sampling (ICGPS), which uses modern generative models that are meta-trained offline and deployed online by in-context autoregressive generation. Theoretically, we show that the Bayesian regret of ICGPS with a learned completion kernel is bounded by the Bayesian regret of a TS benchmark with the ideal completion kernel plus a deployment penalty scaling as $\sqrt{T}$ times the square root of the completion mismatch. This yields a plug-in template for operational problems with known TS regret bounds. For R-NV, we derive sublinear Bayesian regret by reducing censored feedback to bandit convex optimization feedback. We also show that, under reasonable coverage and stability assumptions, the online completion mismatch is controlled by the offline censored predictive mismatch, so offline predictive quality transfers to online performance. Practically, we instantiate ICGPS with ChronosFlow, which combines a frozen time-series transformer backbone with a trainable conditional normalizing-flow head for fast censoring-consistent sampling. In benchmark experiments, ChronosFlow-ICGPS matches correctly specified TS, outperforms myopic and UCB-style baselines, and is robust to prior mismatch and distribution shift. ChronosFlow-ICGPS also performs well for the real-world SuperStore dataset, especially under heavy censoring.

### [43] [TILT: Target-induced loss tilting under covariate shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14280)
*Kakei Yamamoto,Martin J. Wainwright*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出TILT方法，通过分解源域预测器为f+b，在源域监督学习的同时对无标签目标域数据上的辅助组件b施加惩罚，实现无监督域适应。该方法在总体水平上隐式实现相对重要性加权，且b*_f对当前误差自定位并有界。实验表明TILT优于源域单独训练、精确重要性加权和相对密度比基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在协变量偏移下的无监督域适应中，传统重要性加权方法在源域和目标域支撑集不重叠时失效，且加权估计量方差大。需要一种新的目标函数来稳定地实现域适应。

Method: 将源域预测器分解为f+b两部分，在标记源数据上拟合f+b的同时，对未标记目标数据上的辅助组件b施加惩罚。最终部署f作为目标预测器。该方法在总体水平上隐式实现相对重要性加权，且b*_f对当前误差自定位并保持有界。

Result: 在总体水平上证明了目标侧惩罚隐式诱导了相对重要性加权，且b*_f对当前误差自定位，对任何源-目标对（包括支撑集不交叠的情况）一致有界。证明了关于超额风险的有限样本oracle不等式，并给出了稀疏ReLU网络的端到端保证。在受控回归问题和偏移CIFAR-100蒸馏实验中，TILT在目标域性能上优于源域单独训练、精确重要性加权和相对密度比基线，且对正则化参数具有稳定依赖性。

Conclusion: TILT通过预测器分解+目标侧惩罚的新颖策略，有效解决了协变量偏移下无监督域适应问题，特别是在支撑集不重叠的困难场景下仍能保持稳定性能，理论上有有限样本保证，实验上超越现有基线方法。

Abstract: We introduce and analyze Target-Induced Loss Tilting (TILT) for unsupervised domain adaptation under covariate shift. It is based on a novel objective function that decomposes the source predictor as $f+b$, fits $f+b$ on labeled source data while simultaneously penalizing the auxiliary component $b$ on unlabeled target inputs. The resulting fit $f$ is deployed as the final target predictor. At the population level, we show that this target-side penalty implicitly induces relative importance weighting at the population level, but in terms of an estimand $b^*_f$ that is self-localized to the current error, and remains uniformly bounded for any source-target pair (even those with disjoint supports). We prove a general finite-sample oracle inequality on the excess risk, and use it to give an end-to-end guarantee for training with sparse ReLU networks. Experiments on controlled regression problems and shifted CIFAR-100 distillation show that TILT improves target-domain performance over source-only training, exact importance weighting, and relative density-ratio baselines, with a stable dependence on the regularization parameter.

<details>

Method: (i) 利用时间重标定定理（TRT）作为可学习双射，将事件序列映射为i.i.d.单位速率指数噪声；(ii) 三种高效的累积强度参数化方法，可扩展到长序列；(iii) 基于Transformer的编码器，支持多数据集预训练。

Conclusion: SurF是向异步事件流基础模型迈出的初步一步，展示了跨数据集预训练的可行性和有效性。

Abstract: Irregularly sampled multivariate event streams remain a stubbornly difficult modality for generative modeling: tokenization-based approaches break down when inter-event intervals vary by orders of magnitude, and neural temporal point processes are bottlenecked by window-level numerical quadrature. We (i) propose SurF, a generative model that uses the Time Rescaling Theorem (TRT) as a learnable bijection between event sequences and i.i.d.\ unit-rate exponential noise, enabling a single model to be trained across heterogeneous event-stream datasets; (ii) three efficient parameterizations of the cumulative intensity that scale to long sequences; and (iii) a Transformer-based encoder for multi-dataset pretraining. On six real-world benchmarks, SurF achieves the best reported time RMSE on Earthquake, Retweet, and Taobao, and is within trial-level noise of the strongest specialist on the remaining three. Under a strict leave-one-out protocol, the held-out checkpoint beats every classical and neural-autoregressive baseline on 5/6 datasets and beats every baseline on Amazon and Earthquake, an initial step toward foundation models over asynchronous event streams.
